No. 2312/10 – TUESDAY, DECEMBER  27, 2022

1A – PG6122 – 07 (12/2022)
PRADESHIYA  SABHA  PANDUWASNUWARA
IT is hereby notiﬁ ed for the public information that it has been adopted under t he resolution number 05/VIII moved at the 
General Conference held on 13/12/2022 at Pradeshiya Sabha Panduwasnuwara that all the roads and thoroughfares for which 
legal action had not been ﬁ led in a proper judicial Court before the date speciﬁ ed or roads and thoroughfares conﬁ rmed as the 
roads and thoroughfares that should be owned by pradeshiya Sabha panduwasnuwara as per the Decree of a Judicial Court 
in which a case had been ﬁ led before the said date and not mentioned in the following sc hedule from among the roads and 
thoroughfares given in the list of the schedule of the notiﬁ cation published in the Extraordinary Gazette Paper No. 2290/18  and 
dated 27th  July 2022 Shall be conﬁ rmed as roads and thoroughfares owned by the Pradeshiya Sabha Padnuwasnuwara in terms 
of orders made by the series of ‘‘Orders’’ on publication of notiﬁ cations specifying preparation of plans and lists for roads and 
thoroughfares maintained by the pradeshiya Sabha within the North Western Province’’ published by Extraordinary Gazette 
Paper No. 2238/35 and dated 30th July 2021 by the Hon. Governor in the North Western Province and in terms of the order by 
Section 24(1) of Pradeshiya Sabha Act No. 15 of  1987
 It is Further notiﬁ  ed that a list of said roads and thoroughfares has been included in the schedule hereto and all the roads 
and thoroughfares mentioned in that schedule shall be considered as roads and thoroughfares owned by the Pradeshiya Sabha 
Panduwasnuwara under Sub Section (5) of Section 24 of Pradeshiya Sabha Act. 
    
 B. M. Dඁൺඋආൺඌൾඇൺ Bൺආඎඇඎඌංඇ඀ඁൾ,
 Chairman,
 Pradeshiya Sabha, Panduwasnuwara.
 At Panduwasnuwara Pradeshiya Sabha,
Head Oﬃ  ce,
19th of Desember, 2022.

Pൺඋඍ IV (B) – GAZETTE EXTRAORDINARY OF THE DEMOCRATIC SOCIALIST REPUBLIC OF S RI LANKA  – 27.12.2022
 2A
Resolution 
Pradeshiya Sabha Panduwasnuwara Proposes that the roads and tho roughfares for which legal actions had not been ﬁ  led 
in a proper Judicial Court and not mentioned in the following s chedule from among the roads and thoroughfares given in 
the list of the schedule of the notiﬁ cation published in the Extraordinary Gazette Paper No. 2290/18 and dated 27/07/2022 
according to the resolution No. 05-VIII made at the Pradeshiya Sabha conference held on 13/12/2022, shall be conﬁ rmed 
as roads and thoroughfares owned by the Pradeshiya Sabha Panduw asnuwara in terms of orders made by the series of 
“ Orders on publication of notiﬁ cations specifying preparation of plans and lists for roads and thoroughfares maintained by 
the Pradeshiya Sabha within the North Western Province” published by Extraordinary Gazette Paper No. 2238/35 and dated 
30th July 2021 by the Hon. Governor in the North Western Province and in terms of the order by Section 24(1) of Pradeshiya 
Sabha Act No. 15 of 1987,
